Porcupine works the night shift in a warehouse. Each night he gets instructions about where the crates should go. Then he just has to push them into place. Sounds easy, right?\r\n\r\nThe style of the puzzles in Pepe Porcupine originates from a Japanese game called Sokoban. Sokoban means warehouse keeper in Japanese ((ÂÄâÂ∫´Áï™ s≈çkoban).  Sokoban is a type of transport puzzle, in which the player pushes boxes or crates around in a warehouse, trying to get them to storage locations. The game is played on a board of squares, where each square is a floor or a wall.
